[90m15:52:31:283[0m [34m[client-request-interceptor:on][0m adding "request" event listener: async ({ request, requestId, controller }) => {
        const response = await handleRequest(
          request,
          requestId,
          this.handlersController.currentHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("RequestHandler")),
          this.resolvedOptions,
          this.emitter,
          {
            onPassthroughResponse(request2) {
              const acceptHeader = request2.headers.get("accept");
              if (acceptHeader) {
                const nextAcceptHeader = acceptHeader.replace(
                  /(,\s+)?msw\/passthrough/,
                  ""
                );
                if (nextAcceptHeader) {
                  request2.headers.set("accept", nextAcceptHeader);
                } else {
                  request2.headers.delete("accept");
                }
              }
            }
          }
        );
        if (response) {
          controller.respondWith(response);
        }
        return;
      }

[90m15:52:31:284[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }

    });

[90m15:52:31:765[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }

[90m15:52:32:192[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }

[90m15:52:32:194[0m [34m[client-request-interceptor:on][0m adding "request" event listener: async ({ request, requestId, controller }) => {
        const response = await handleRequest(
          request,
          requestId,
          this.handlersController.currentHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("RequestHandler")),
          this.resolvedOptions,
          this.emitter,
          {
            onPassthroughResponse(request2) {
              const acceptHeader = request2.headers.get("accept");
              if (acceptHeader) {
                const nextAcceptHeader = acceptHeader.replace(
                  /(,\s+)?msw\/passthrough/,
                  ""
                );
                if (nextAcceptHeader) {
                  request2.headers.set("accept", nextAcceptHeader);
                } else {
                  request2.headers.delete("accept");
                }
              }
            }
          }
        );
        if (response) {
          controller.respondWith(response);
        }
        return;
      }

[90m15:52:32:246[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }

    });

              }
            }
          }

        }
        return;
      }

[90m15:52:37:200[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }

[90m15:52:37:485[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }

[90m15:52:40:455[0m [34m[client-request-interceptor:on][0m adding "request" event listener: async ({ request, requestId, controller }) => {
        const response = await handleRequest(
          request,
          requestId,
          this.handlersController.currentHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("RequestHandler")),
          this.resolvedOptions,
          this.emitter,
          {
            onPassthroughResponse(request2) {
              const acceptHeader = request2.headers.get("accept");
              if (acceptHeader) {
                const nextAcceptHeader = acceptHeader.replace(
                  /(,\s+)?msw\/passthrough/,
                  ""
                );
                if (nextAcceptHeader) {
                  request2.headers.set("accept", nextAcceptHeader);
                } else {
                  request2.headers.delete("accept");
                }
              }
            }
          }
        );
        if (response) {
          controller.respondWith(response);
        }
        return;
      }

[90m15:52:40:456[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }

    });

[90m15:52:41:490[0m [34m[client-request-interceptor:on][0m adding "request" event listener: async ({ request, requestId, controller }) => {
        const response = await handleRequest(
          request,
          requestId,
          this.handlersController.currentHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("RequestHandler")),
          this.resolvedOptions,
          this.emitter,
          {
            onPassthroughResponse(request2) {
              const acceptHeader = request2.headers.get("accept");
              if (acceptHeader) {
                const nextAcceptHeader = acceptHeader.replace(
                  /(,\s+)?msw\/passthrough/,
                  ""
                );
                if (nextAcceptHeader) {
                  request2.headers.set("accept", nextAcceptHeader);
                } else {
                  request2.headers.delete("accept");
                }
              }
            }
          }
        );
        if (response) {
          controller.respondWith(response);
        }

[90m15:52:41:492[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }

              }

[90m15:52:42:124[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }

        const response = await handleRequest(
          request,
          requestId,
          this.handlersController.currentHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("RequestHandler")),
          this.resolvedOptions,
          this.emitter,
          {
            onPassthroughResponse(request2) {
              const acceptHeader = request2.headers.get("accept");
              if (acceptHeader) {
                const nextAcceptHeader = acceptHeader.replace(
                  /(,\s+)?msw\/passthrough/,
                  ""
                );
                if (nextAcceptHeader) {
                  request2.headers.set("accept", nextAcceptHeader);
                } else {
                  request2.headers.delete("accept");
                }
              }
            }
          }
        );
        if (response) {
          controller.respondWith(response);
        }
        return;
      }

[90m15:52:43:139[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }

                }
              }
            }
          }
        );

        }
        return;
      }

[90m15:52:43:485[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }

[90m15:52:44:564[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }

              }

          }
        );

        }
        return;
      }

[90m15:52:45:522[0m [34m[websocket:on][0m adding "connection" event listener: async (connection) => {
    const handlers = options.getHandlers().filter(isHandlerKind("EventHandler"));
    if (handlers.length > 0) {
      options?.onMockedConnection(connection);
      await Promise.all(
        handlers.map((handler) => {
          return handler.run(connection);
        })
      );
      return;
    }
    const request = new Request(connection.client.url, {
      headers: {
        upgrade: "websocket",
        connection: "upgrade"
      }
    });
    await onUnhandledRequest(
      request,
      options.getUnhandledRequestStrategy()
    ).catch((error) => {
      const errorEvent = new Event("error");
      Object.defineProperty(errorEvent, "cause", {
        enumerable: true,
        configurable: false,
        value: error
      });
      connection.client.socket.dispatchEvent(errorEvent);
    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
    connection.server.connect();
  }

        enumerable: true,

      });

    });
    options?.onPassthroughConnection(connection);
